def replace_char(string, char, new_char):
    '''Replace the character in a string with a new character.
    
    Args:
        string (str): The string to be replaced.
        char (str): The character to be replaced.
        new_char (str): The new character to be replaced.

        str: The string with the character replaced.

'''Write a function to replace characters in a string.'''
def replace_char(string, char, new_char):
    '''Replace the character in a string with a new character.
    
    Args:
        string (str): The string to be replaced.
        char (str): The character to be replaced.
        new_char (str): The new character to be replaced.
    
    Returns:
        str: The string with the character replaced.
    '''
    return string.replace(char, new_char)


# Test
